150      "model_formulas = {\n", 
151      "    \"m1\": \"price ~ km\",\n", 
152      "    \"m2\": \"price ~ age\",\n", 
153      "    \"m3\": \"price ~ km + age\",\n", 
154      "    \"m4\": \"price ~ km + age + km10 + power_lowest + power_low + power_mid + power_high + \"\n", 
155      "          \"power_highest + ba + bb + ke + nr + po + tn + tt + petrol + petgas + man + eng1 + \"\n", 
156      "          \"eng2 + eng3 + eng4 + eng6\",\n", 
157      "    \"m5\": \"price ~ km + I(km**2) + age + I(age**2) + diesel + man + eng1 + eng2 + eng3 + eng4 + eng6\"\n", 
158      "}" 
159     ], 
160     "metadata": { 
161      "collapsed": false, 
162      "pycharm": { 
163       "name": "#%%\n" 
164      } 
165     }

167    {

170      "The following function iterates over all models and returns the fitted objects" 
171     ], 
172     "metadata": { 
173      "collapsed": false,

175       "name": "#%% md\n" 
176      } 
177     }

179    { 
180     "cell_type": "code", 
181     "execution_count": 20, 
182     "outputs": [], 
183     "source": [ 
184      "def fit_ols_models(models_specs: dict, data: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:\n", 
185      "    \"\"\"\n", 
186      "    Purpose: For the specified formulas, fit the OLS model and return all its attributes\n", 
187      "    \"\"\"\n", 
188      "\n", 
189      "    models_fitted = {}\n", 
190      "    for model, formula in models_specs.items():\n", 
191      "        models_fitted[model] = smf.ols(formula=formula, data=data).fit()\n", 
192      "\n", 
193      "    return models_fitted" 
194     ], 
195     "metadata": { 
196      "collapsed": false, 
197      "pycharm": { 
198       "name": "#%%\n" 
199      } 
200     } 
201    }, 
202    { 
203     "cell_type": "code", 
204     "execution_count": 24, 
205     "outputs": [], 
206     "source": [ 
207      "models_res = fit_ols_models(model_formulas, ocr)  # object containing all fitted models" 
208     ],

233      "def print_models_summary(models_res_list: dict) -> None:\n", 
234      "    \"\"\"\n", 
235      "    Purpose: Print summary tables for each model from the dictionary of fitted models\n", 
236      "    \"\"\"\n", 
237      "\n", 
238      "    for mod, res in models_res_list.items():\n", 
239      "        print(f\"{mod}:\\n\\n \"\n", 
240      "              f\"Coefficients: \\n\"\n", 
241      "              f\"{res.summary()} \\n\\n\")"

487      "def generate_predictions(models_fitted: dict, data_test: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:\n", 
488      "    \"\"\"\n", 
489      "    Purpose: For all fitted models, generate predictions for the test set and store them in a dictionary\n", 
490      "    \"\"\"\n", 
491      "    pred_vals = {}\n", 
492      "    for model, specs in models_fitted.items():\n", 
493      "        pred_vals[model] = specs.predict(data_test)\n", 
494      "\n", 
495      "    return pred_vals" 
496     ], 
497     "metadata": { 
498      "collapsed": false, 
499      "pycharm": { 
500       "name": "#%%\n" 
501      } 
502     } 
503    },

521      "We can plot the actual values in our test set against the predictions. This has the same effect as the residual analysis.\n", 
522      "We can therefore check if the predicitons substantially differ for different values of our target variable" 
523     ],

535     "source": [ 
536      "from sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error as mse\n", 
537      "def compare_models_metrics(preds_dict, data_observed, metric, print_res=False):\n", 
538      "\n", 
539      "    metric_dict = {}\n", 
540      "\n", 
541      "    for mod, fit in preds_dict.items():\n", 
542      "        metric_dict[mod] = metric(preds_dict[mod], data_observed)\n", 
543      "        # metric_dict[mod] = mse(data_observed, preds_dict[mod])\n", 
544      "\n", 
545      "    if print_res:\n", 
546      "        for key, val in sorted(metric_dict.items(), key = lambda x: x[1], reverse=False) :\n", 
547      "            print(f\"Model {key} had the metric score of of: {val}\\n\")\n", 
548      "\n", 
549      "    return metric_dict" 
550     ],

594      "def get_grid_shape(data):\n", 
595      "    \"\"\"\n", 
596      "    Purpose: Helper function to create a tupe which would determine the subplots shape\n", 
597      "    \"\"\"\n", 
598      "    grid_size = (math.ceil(np.sqrt(len(data))), math.floor(np.sqrt(len(data))))\n", 
599      "\n", 
600      "    return grid_size" 
601     ], 
602     "metadata": { 
603      "collapsed": false, 
604      "pycharm": { 
605       "name": "#%%\n"

613     "source": [ 
614      "def actual_vs_fit_plot(fitted, actuals, mse):\n", 
615      "    \"\"\"\n", 
616      "    Purpose: Generate scatter plots to plot the actual values against the fitted ones\n", 
617      "    \"\"\"\n", 
618      "    shape = get_grid_shape(fitted)\n", 
619      "\n", 
620      "    fig, axs = plt.subplots(shape[0], shape[1], figsize=tuple([5*x for x in shape]))\n", 
621      "    fig.suptitle(\"Actual vs. Fitted values Regression Plot\")\n", 
622      "    i = 0\n", 
623      "    j = 0\n", 
624      "    for model, vals in fitted.items():\n", 
625      "        sns.regplot(ax=axs[i, j % 2], x=vals, y=actuals, line_kws={'color': 'red'})\n", 
626      "        axs[i, j % 2].set_title(f\"{model}: MSE of {round(mse[model])}\")\n", 
627      "        i = i + j\n", 
628      "        j = (j + 1) % 2" 
629     ], 
630     "metadata": { 
631      "collapsed": false, 
632      "pycharm": { 
633       "name": "#%%\n" 
634      }

685      "At first, I initialize the functionction which is meant to extract the coefficients of our regression"

697     "outputs": [], 
698     "source": [ 
699      "def est_model(data, formula):\n", 
700      "    # bootstrap() makes an array, not a DataFrame\n", 
701      "    estimate = smf.ols(formula, data).fit()\n", 
702      "    coefs = estimate.params\n", 
703      "\n", 
704      "    return coefs" 
705     ], 
706     "metadata": { 
707      "collapsed": false, 
708      "pycharm": { 
709       "name": "#%%\n" 
710      } 
711     } 
712    }, 
713    { 
714     "cell_type": "code", 
715     "execution_count": null, 
716     "outputs": [], 
717     "source": [ 
718      "def get_bootstrap_coefs(data, n_rep, formula):\n", 
719      "    res = []\n", 
720      "\n", 
721      "    for i in range(n_rep):\n", 
722      "        smpl = data.sample(frac=1, replace=True)\n", 
723      "        model = smf.ols(formula, smpl).fit()\n", 
724      "        coefs = model.params\n", 
725      "\n", 
726      "        res.append(coefs)\n", 
727      "\n", 
728      "    return pd.DataFrame(res, columns=coefs.index)\n" 
729     ], 
730     "metadata": { 
731      "collapsed": false, 
732      "pycharm": { 
733       "name": "#%%\n" 
734      } 
735     } 
736    },

743     ],

756      "def get_quantiles(data, q_list = [0.01, 0.5, 0.99]):\n", 
757      "\n", 
758      "    df_q = data.quantile(q_list).set_index(pd.Index([q for q in q_list])).transpose()\n", 
759      "\n", 
760      "    return df_q"

769    { 
770     "cell_type": "code", 
771     "execution_count": null, 
772     "outputs": [], 
773     "source": [ 
774      "def get_stats(data, alpha, q_list):\n", 
775      "\n", 
776      "    stats_dict = {\n", 
777      "        'mean': data.mean(),\n", 
778      "        'std': data.std(),\n", 
779      "        'se': data.std()/np.sqrt(data.shape[0]),\n", 
780      "        't_stat': stats.t.ppf(q=1 - alpha/2, df=data.shape[0] - 1),\n", 
781      "        'quantiles': data.quantile(q_list).set_index(pd.Index([q for q in q_list])).transpose()\n", 
782      "    }\n", 
783      "\n", 
784      "    return stats_dict\n", 
785      "\n", 
786      "\n" 
787     ],
